+ "\n\nDescription: \""
+ "\n    /* Excluded is equal or higher priority, take */\n    ELSE "
+ "\n    /* Existing is higher priority, keep */\n    WHEN persistent_tasks.reason_priority > excluded.reason_priority THEN "
